  <script type="text/javascript">
var o2ViewsFrontSidePost = o2.Views.FrontSidePost;
o2.Views.FrontSidePost = ( function( $ ) {
	return o2ViewsFrontSidePost.extend( {
		isPostTypeSelected: false,

		// Add event listener for select menu.
		events: function() {
			return _.extend( {
				'change #polyglots-post-type': 'onPostTypeChange'
			}, o2ViewsFrontSidePost.prototype.events );
		},

		// Prevent saving when no post type is selected.
		onSave: function( event ) {
			if ( ! this.isPostTypeSelected ) {
				return false;
			}

			o2ViewsFrontSidePost.prototype.onSave.apply( this, arguments );
		},

		// Event listener for select menu.
		onPostTypeChange: function( event ) {
			this.isPostTypeSelected = ( '-1' !== $( event.target ).val() );
			this.toggleSaveButtonStatus();
		},

		// Toggle active status of save button.
		toggleSaveButtonStatus: function() {
			var $button = this.$el.find( '.o2-save' );
			if ( this.isPostTypeSelected ) {
				$button
					.removeClass( 'disabled' )
					.removeAttr( 'tabindex' );
			} else {
				$button
					.addClass( 'disabled' )
					.attr( 'tabindex', -1 );
			}
		},

		// Call parent render() method and render status of save button.
		render: function() {
			o2ViewsFrontSidePost.prototype.render.apply( this, arguments );
			this.isPostTypeSelected = ( '-1' !== this.$el.find( '#polyglots-post-type' ).val() );
			this.toggleSaveButtonStatus();
			return this;
		}
	} );
} )( jQuery );
</script>

        c = m.className;

  <div class="make-welcome"> 
   <div class="entry-meta"> 
    <button type="button" id="make-welcome-hide" class="toggle dashicons dashicons-no" data-hash="025440d3f5804496cfc4444fce2bc96b" data-cookie="welcome-19" title="Hide this message"></button> 
   </div> 
   <div class="entry-content clear"> 
    <div class="column welcome"> 
     <p>Welcome to the official blog of the translators team for the WordPress open source project.</p> 
     <p>This is where we discuss all things related to translating WordPress. Follow our progress for general updates, status reports, and debates.</p> 
     <p>We’d love for you to help out.</p> 
    </div> 
    <div class="column"> 
     <h4>Translate WordPress</h4> 
     <p>You can help translating WordPress to your language at any time. Just <a href="https://login.wordpress.org/wp-login.php?redirect_to=https%3A%2F%2Ftranslate.wordpress.org%2F">log in to the translation platform with your WordPress.org account</a>,&nbsp;and suggest translations. If you want to help in managing and validating translations, please make sure to get in touch with the <strong><a href="https://make.wordpress.org/polyglots/teams/">existing language team</a></strong> first.</p> 
     <h4>Don’t see your language?</h4> 
     <p>Request support for it by following <strong><a href="https://make.wordpress.org/polyglots/handbook/translating/requesting-a-new-locale/">this guide</a></strong>. We’ll have you up and running in no time.</p> 
    </div> 
    <div class="column"> 
     <h4>Weekly Meetings</h4> 
     <p>We have two weekly meetings on Slack in <a href="https://make.wordpress.org/polyglots/tag/polyglots/" class="tag"><span class="tag-prefix">#</span>polyglots</a>, on <a href="http://www.timeanddate.com/worldclock/fixedtime.html?iso=20171004T0600"><abbr class="date" title="2017-10-04T06:00:00+00:00">Wednesday 06:00 UTC</abbr></a> and <a href="http://www.timeanddate.com/worldclock/fixedtime.html?iso=20171004T1000"><abbr class="date" title="2017-10-04T10:00:00+00:00">Wednesday 10:00 UTC</abbr></a>. If you have any questions, bring them to the weekly chats!</p> 
     <h4>Posting here</h4> 
     <p>In order to post to this site, you will need to <a href="https://login.wordpress.org/wp-login.php?redirect_to=https%3A%2F%2Fmake.wordpress.org%2Fpolyglots%2F">log in with your wordpress.org account</a>. Your first post may take a while to show up, as it is moderated. Please follow our <strong><a href="https://make.wordpress.org/polyglots/tag-policy/">tag policy</a></strong> when posting.</p> 
    </div>
    <nav class="o2-post-footer-actions">
     <ul class="o2-post-footer-action-row"></ul>
     <div class="o2-post-footer-action-likes"></div>
     <ul class="o2-post-footer-action-row"></ul>
    </nav>

      <header class="page-header"> 
       <h1 class="page-title"> Translation Teams <span class="controls"> </span> </h1> 
       <span class="entry-actions"> </span> 
      </header>
      <!-- .page-header --> 
      <article id="post-5032" class="post-5032 page type-page status-publish hentry author-nacin"> 
       <div class="entry-content"> 
        <p>Below is a list of languages WordPress supports. Each translation team below works to translate WordPress into their language. If you are interested in helping them translate WordPress or other related projects, please read the <a href="https://make.wordpress.org/polyglots/handbook/">Translator Handbook</a> or contact the translation editor(s) for your language using the “Team” link.</p> 
        <p>Note that some translations teams have fully translated WordPress into their language, while others are not yet complete. This page tracks the progress of translation teams.</p> 
        <hr> 
        <p>&nbsp;</p> 
        <div class="translators-info show-all"> 
         <p class="locale-filters"> Releases: <a href="#all" class="i18n-filter" data-filter="all"><strong class="i18n-label all">169</strong> locales.</a> <a href="#latest" class="i18n-filter" data-filter="latest"><strong class="i18n-label latest">8</strong> locales up to date.</a> <a href="#minor-behind" class="i18n-filter" data-filter="minor-behind"><strong class="i18n-label minor-behind">57</strong> locales behind by minor versions.</a> <a href="#major-behind-one" class="i18n-filter" data-filter="major-behind-one"><strong class="i18n-label major-behind-one">30</strong> locales behind by one major version.</a> <a href="#major-behind-many" class="i18n-filter" data-filter="major-behind-many"><strong class="i18n-label major-behind-many">14</strong> locales behind more than one major version.</a> <a href="#no-releases" class="i18n-filter" data-filter="no-releases"><strong class="i18n-label no-releases">51</strong> locales have a site but never released.</a> <a href="#no-site" class="i18n-filter" data-filter="no-site"><strong class="i18n-label no-site">9</strong> locales don’t have a site.</a> </p> 
         <p class="locale-filters"> Translations: <a href="#all" class="i18n-filter" data-filter="all"><strong class="i18n-label all">169</strong> locales.</a> <a href="#translated-100" class="i18n-filter" data-filter="translated-100"><strong class="i18n-label translated-100">63</strong> locales at 100%.</a> <a href="#translated-95" class="i18n-filter" data-filter="translated-95"><strong class="i18n-label translated-95">13</strong> locales have more than 95%.</a> <a href="#translated-90" class="i18n-filter" data-filter="translated-90"><strong class="i18n-label translated-90">2</strong> locales have more than 90%.</a> <a href="#translated-50" class="i18n-filter" data-filter="translated-50"><strong class="i18n-label translated-50">28</strong> locales have more than 50%.</a> <a href="#translated-50-less" class="i18n-filter" data-filter="translated-50-less"><strong class="i18n-label translated-50-less">55</strong> locales have less than 50%.</a> <a href="#has-language-pack" class="i18n-filter" data-filter="has-language-pack"><strong class="i18n-label has-language-pack">106</strong> locales have a language pack.</a> <a href="#no-language-pack" class="i18n-filter" data-filter="no-language-pack"><strong class="i18n-label no-language-pack">63</strong> locales have no language pack.</a> <a href="#no-wp-project" class="i18n-filter" data-filter="no-wp-project"><strong class="i18n-label no-wp-project">8</strong> locales don’t have a WP project.</a> </p>

  <script>
				jQuery(document).ready(function($) {
					var bootstrap = { data: [] };
					o2Data = $( '.o2-data' );
					if ( o2Data.length > 0 ) {
						o2Data.each( function() {
							// Parse the JSON that's embedded in the page and add it to the bootstrap data
							var me = $( this );
							var thread;
							try {
								thread = $.parseJSON( me.text() );
							} catch( e ) {
								thread = false;
								console.log( '$.parseJSON failure: ' + me.text() );
							}
							if ( false !== thread ) {
								_.each( thread, function( frag ) {
									bootstrap.data.push( frag );
								} );
							}
							me.remove();
						} );
					}

					// Merge o2Config into o2 itself
					o2 = $.extend( o2, o2Config );

					// Some generally-useful references
					o2.$body = $( 'body' );
					o2.$appContainer = $( o2.options.appContainer );

					// As soon as o2 loads, poll for new content to account
					// for Chrome's caching weirdness on back/tab-recovery.
					o2.$appContainer.on( 'ready.o2', function() {
						o2.Polling.poll();
					} );

					// Bootstrap o2 with any in-page content
					o2.start( bootstrap );
				});
			</script>

		jQuery( document ).ready( function( $ ) {
			var bootstrap = { data: [], found: [] };
			var resolvedPostsData = $( '.o2-resolved-posts-data' );
			if ( resolvedPostsData.length > 0 ) {
				_.each( $.parseJSON( resolvedPostsData.text() ), function( fragment ) {
					bootstrap.data.push( fragment );
				} );
				resolvedPostsData.remove();
			}
			var foundPostsData = $( '.o2-resolved-posts-found' );

					bootstrap.found.push( fragment );
				} );
				foundPostsData.remove();
			}
			o2.startToDos( bootstrap );
		} );

  <script type="text/javascript">
	jQuery(document).ready( function ($) {
		var timestrings = {"months":["January","February","March","April","May","June","July","August","September","October","November","December"],"days":["Sunday","Monday","Tuesday","Wednesday","Thursday","Friday","Saturday"]}
		var parse_date = function (text) {
			var m = /^([0-9]{4})-([0-9]{2})-([0-9]{2})T([0-9]{2}):([0-9]{2}):([0-9]{2})\+00:00$/.exec(text);
			var d = new Date();
			d.setUTCFullYear(+m[1]);
			d.setUTCDate(+m[3]);
			d.setUTCMonth(+m[2]-1);
			d.setUTCHours(+m[4]);
			d.setUTCMinutes(+m[5]);
			d.setUTCSeconds(+m[6]);
			return d;
		}
		var format_time = function (d) {
			return d.toLocaleTimeString(navigator.language, {weekday: 'long', month: 'long', day: 'numeric', year: 'numeric', hour: '2-digit', minute:'2-digit', timeZoneName: 'short'});
		}
		var format_date = function (d) {
			return d.toLocaleDateString(navigator.language, {weekday: 'long', month: 'long', day: 'numeric', year: 'numeric'});
		}
		/* Not all browsers, particularly Safari, support arguments to .toLocaleTimeString(). */
		var toLocaleTimeStringSupportsLocales = (function() {
			try {
				new Date().toLocaleTimeString('i');
			} catch (e) {
				return e.name === 'RangeError';
			}
			return false;
		})();
		var nodes = document.getElementsByTagName('abbr');
		for (var i=0; i<nodes.length; ++i) {
			var node = nodes[i];
			if (node.className === 'date') {
				var d = parse_date(node.getAttribute('title'));
				if (d) {
					var new_text = '';
					if ( ! toLocaleTimeStringSupportsLocales ) {
						new_text += format_date(d);
						new_text += ' ';
					}
					new_text += format_time(d);
					node.textContent = new_text;
				}
			}
		}
	});
	</script>
